

.. Nationality:

Nationality
====================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================

Population breakdowns by nationality and place of birth.

.. contents::
   :local:
   :depth: 10





.. _ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t003c002_f:

Total population - Canadian citizens (female)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------











Measure "Total population - Canadian citizens (female)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t003c002_f'
      );





Measure "Total population - Canadian citizens (female)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

    UPDATE {table_name}
      SET {new_numeric_column} =
        OBS_GetMeasure(
          ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307), 0.01),
          'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t003c002_f'
        );






Measure "Total population - Canadian citizens (female)" percent of "Total population in private households (female)" at one point:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t003c002_f',
        'denominator'
      );


Measure "Total population - Canadian citizens (female)" percent of "Total population in private households (female)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307), 0.01),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t003c002_f',
        'denominator'
      );

.. _ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t024c001_m:

Total recent immigrant population in private households by selected places of birth (male)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------





Recent immigrants are immigrants who landed in Canada since the last census survey





Measure "Total recent immigrant population in private households by selected places of birth (male)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t024c001_m'
      );

        );

.. _ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t024c001_t:

Total recent immigrant population in private households by selected places of birth (total)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------





Recent immigrants are immigrants who landed in Canada since the last census survey





Measure "Total recent immigrant population in private households by selected places of birth (total)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t024c001_t'
      );
